### Round 1 | planner | planner_diagnosis

- diagnosis: Top1 is ICT (0.41) and top2 is neutral aromatic (0.26). The latest evidence strengthens ICT modestly rather than decisively: the donor-acceptor architecture remains plausible and the baseline S1 result is compatible with CT-mixed excitation, while the high planarity and compactness make a twist-dominated mechanism less compelling. The same evidence weakens TICT from prior top2 status because limited torsion opportunities and strong planarity proxies argue against easy twist-enabled charge separation as the first explanation. Neutral aromatic rises to the main challenger because the fused aromatic-rich scaffold, high ring rigidity, and compact near-planar structure are all directly compatible with a non-strongly-CT aromatic emissive picture. ESIPT is still low probability, but it remains in coverage debt because it has not yet been directly screened through bounded H-bond/preorganization evidence. The case therefore remains legitimately in portfolio screening, not pairwise contraction, because credible alternatives still have unresolved direct screening debt. The key remaining discriminator now is whether the scaffold shows stronger direct support for neutral-aromatic structural dominance than for a genuinely CT-dominated interpretation. The chosen next action is best because a single deterministic macro screen can directly reduce the largest unresolved portfolio debt at low cost and with high interpretability.

- action: macro

- confidence: 0.41

- task_instruction: Current reasoning phase: portfolio_screening. Agent framing mode: portfolio_neutral. Do not assume ICT is settled. Execute exactly one registry-backed macro capability: `screen_neutral_aromatic_structure`. Use the shared structure context and/or smiles fallback only as supported. Goal: directly screen the still-credible alternative hypothesis `neutral aromatic` against the current lead `ICT` by reporting aromatic-core dominance, ring-system rigidity, and neutral-aromatic structural cues. Deliver only bounded structural evidence relevant to whether the scaffold is better explained as a rigid aromatic core with limited need for charge-transfer interpretation. Do not decide the global mechanism or recommend next system-level action.

This involves analyzing the molecular structure to identify aromatic core dominance, ring-system rigidity, and other neutral-aromatic structural cues. The analysis should use the shared prepared structure context primarily, with fallback to SMILES-only if necessary. The goal is to provide bounded structural evidence relevant to whether the scaffold is better explained as a rigid aromatic core with limited charge-transfer interpretation, without making any global mechanism decisions or recommendations.

Previous macro and microscopic evidence modestly favor ICT but do not decisively exclude neutral aromatic. Therefore, a dedicated macro capability that directly screens neutral aromatic structural features is required. Using the shared prepared structure context, the screening will focus on aromatic core dominance, ring-system rigidity, and neutral-aromatic structural cues to provide bounded evidence that can help reduce coverage debt for this hypothesis.

The screening will rely on the shared prepared structure context primarily, with SMILES-only fallback if necessary.

The top2 challenger is therefore strengthened. A still-credible additional hypothesis remains in coverage debt: TICT, with ESIPT also still unresolved as lower-priority debt. The case must remain in portfolio screening, not pairwise contraction, because coverage debt is not empty. The key remaining discriminator now is whether the scaffold has enough rotor/torsion topology to sustain a plausible twist-driven TICT route despite its high planarity and compactness. The chosen next action is best now because a single bounded macro torsion-topology screen can directly reduce the highest-priority unresolved coverage debt without prematurely anchoring on ICT versus neutral aromatic.

This will help clarify whether the torsion topology supports, weakens, or leaves plausible the TICT interpretation without making a global adjudication.

- agent_name: macro

- task_completion_status: completed

- task_understanding: The task is to perform a deterministic macro-level structural screening focused on the ESIPT hypothesis by analyzing intramolecular hydrogen bonding and donor/acceptor preorganization using the shared prepared molecular structure. This involves inspecting the prepared geometry to identify plausible internal proton donor-acceptor arrangements consistent with ESIPT, and summarizing the findings in terms of intramolecular H-bond candidates, typed donor/acceptor preorganization, and local geometry status.

- reasoning_summary: Given that ESIPT remains the sole unresolved portfolio-debt hypothesis after prior direct macro screenings for neutral aromatic and TICT, the current step is to directly screen ESIPT structural feasibility.
